The data returned by this endpoint is fairly large (more than 5MB) since it includes vods from 2015 up to (at the time of writing this) June 2019 and it will continue growing. Do consider this when dealing with clients (like mobile phones) where bandwidth and memory may be scarce. It is highly advised that you cache the data from this endpoint. |
